##Synopsis

##Loading and Processing the Raw Data

Using Storm Data from the U.S. National Oceanic and Atmospheric Administrationâ€™s (NOAA) storm database, we analyze conditions that impact the health of human populations throughout the US.

###Data Processing

###Downloading and reading a small sample of the data for column names and early classification. 

temp <- tempfile()
download.file("https://d396qusza40orc.cloudfront.net/repdata%2Fdata%2FStormData.csv.bz2", 
              temp, method = "auto", mode = "wb")
sdata <- read.table(bzfile(temp), comment.char = "#", header = TRUE, sep = ",", nrows = 10, 
                    na.strings = "", )
dim(sdata)

## [1] 10 37

# rawnames <- readLines(bzfile(temp), 1)

###Read all the data Some of the column classes are not interpreted correctly. Read in a larger chunk of data as character classes then reclassify the columns after examination.

sdata <- read.table(bzfile(temp), comment.char = "#", header = TRUE, sep = ",", nrows = 1000,
                    colClasses = "character", na.strings = "", )
names(sdata) <- cnames
dim(sdata)

## [1] 1000   37
